RTCore64.sys

Description

RTCore64.sys is a vulnerable driver and more information will be added as found.

  • UUID: 275c80c5-a67c-4536-b29e-4e481242cb01
  • Created: 2023-05-06
  • Author: Nasreddine Bencherchali
  • Acknowledgement: |

DownloadBlock

This download link contains the vulnerable driver!

Commands

sc.exe create RTCore64.sys binPath=C:\windows\temp\RTCore64.sys type=kernel &amp;&amp; sc.exe start RTCore64.sys
Use Case Privileges Operating System
Elevate privileges kernel Windows 10
